Building 214 on the UCI campus map Email mbeyeler uci edu If you send email please put CS 171 somewhere in the Subject line Goal The goal of this class is to familiarize you with the basic principles of artificial intelligence You will learn some basic AI techniques the problems for which they are applicable and their limitations The course content is organized roughly around what are often considered to be three central pillars of AI Search Logic and Learning Topics covered include basic search heuristic search game playing constraint satisfaction knowledge representation logic and inference probabilistic modeling and machine learning algorithms This is a broad introductory survey course We will move rapidly through the basic fundamentals of a large number of AI topics For every topic that we touch there are specialized techniques available to the sophisticated practitioner that will go beyond what we are able to cover in 1 short weeks The bright interested and motivated student is encouraged to pursue advanced studies In any case if you work hard study hard and master the presented material you will emerge from this course with a basic grasp of some of the fundamental methods that we use to engineer intelligent systems Class Setup The course will be primarily lecture based There will be a Mid term and a Final Exam On most second Tuesdays the first 2 minutes will be an in class pop quiz followed by lecture see specific dates in Syllabus below The frequent quizzes are intended to encourage you to stay current with the course material All exams and quizzes may cover all material presented in class including lectures and assigned textbook reading Quizzes will cover mostly material presented since the last quiz and also may include questions that many students missed on the previous quiz The Final Exam will cover mostly material since the Mid term Exam and also will include many questions intended to encourage you to remember the earlier material i e it will be comprehensive Please study the previous CS 171 quizzes and exams below which are made available as study guides to help you learn and master the class material they are important guides about the performance that will be expected from you now There will be an AI coding project see Project section below You are allowed to do the project by yourself or you may form project teams of two students following the Pair Programming paradigm Please note that you are encouraged to discuss concepts methods algorithms etc but you are forbidden to copy 1 source code from any source or 2 text from any source unless properly cited and set off as a quote Except for class materials provided from this class website you must invent and write all of your own code by yourself with your partner Except for properly referenced material you must write all of your own project report by yourself with your partner Please note that your source code and project report are subject to analysis by automated plagiarism detection programs and that direct copying will be treated as an act of academic dishonesty please see the section on Academic Honesty below Please start your AI coding project earlier than you believe necessary it will take longer and be more difficult than you expect as is true of all coding projects everywhere at all times All my AI project shells were written by former CS 171 students who became interested in AI and signed up for CS 199 in order to pursue their interest and write more interesting AI project shells Please let me know if this is of interest to you CS 171 grade of A or better required Homework will be assigned but is not graded The reason is that prior student course evaluations alerted me to the existence of student cheating by way of copying the homework answers I deplore this degree of personal degradation in dishonest students but I cannot control it and so I avoid the opportunity I remain determined to create a fair and honest educational experience for all students as best I can Textbook Required Russell Norvig Artificial Intelligence A Modern Approach 3rd edition The course is based on and the UCI bookstore has the 3rd edition The assigned textbook reading is required and is fair game for quizzes and exams You place yourself at a distinct disadvantage if you do not have the textbook I expect that you have a personal copy of the textbook and quizzes and exams are written accordingly Please purchase or rent your own personal textbook for the quarter and then resell it back to the UCI Bookstore at the end if you don t want it for reference Please do not jeopardize your precious educational experience with the false economy of trying to save a few dollars by not having a personal copy of the textbook Also for your convenience I have requested that a copy of the textbook be placed on reserve in the UCI Science Library There is a two hour check out limit However please understand that with high student enrollments it is unrealistic to expect that these thin reserves will always be available when you need them Please purchase or rent your own personal textbook I do deplore the high cost of textbooks You are likely to find the book cheaper if you search online at EBay com Amazon com and related sites A student kindly contributed this link to a blog that offers a PDF of the course You will be expected to learn and master a large body of technical material in a very short period of time and to demonstrate your mastery by 1 accurate performance on frequent quizzes and exams and 2 successful implementation of an AI coding project Although I deliberately treat you as adults who are responsible for your own educational decisions and so lecture and discussion sections are optional nevertheless students who do not attend lecture or discussion sections are at a serious disadvantage and do not succeed as well in this class They send me emails asking questions that already were covered thoroughly and in detail during lecture and again in discussion section They miss points on quizzes and exams that already have been discussed thoroughly Your educational moments are precious and your education now will be the single most important factor in your future career success or failure Please make the most of your precious educational moments now please attend both lecture and discussion section Please do not ever fall behind in the class material instead study frequently and diligently Please begin your AI coding project earlier than you believe necessary it will take longer and be more difficult than you expect as is true of all coding projects everywhere at all times Please work harder and study longer Please understand thoroughly all class material and ask questions when you do not understand Please attend all lectures and discussion sections Please come to lectures and discussion sections prepared with questions about any material that is not clear Please do all assigned reading both before and again after lecture Please review the lecture notes several times over both before and again after lecture until you understand every detail Please regularly attend office hours with me and the TA Please ask questions about any class material that is not absolutely crystal clear Please work and understand all past quizzes and exams they are Machinery and Intelligence Thu 15 Jan Local Search Read in advance Textbook Chapter 4 1 4 2 Lecture slides two parts 1 Local Search PDF PPT and 2 Representation PDF PPT Optional URLs Hill Climbing with Simulated Annealing Boxcar 2D The program learns to build a car using a genetic algorithm If you let this program run for a long time 3 generations you will see that eventually it produces cars well suited to the terrain This outcome illustrates a general theme of genetic algorithms very very slow but eventually good performance After all it took 3 6 billion years to evolve humans from bacteria http en wikipedia org wiki Timeline of evolutionary history of life Please note that this eventual good performance of genetic algorithms is conditional upon a representation that allows good solutions to sub problems to be combined simply by cross over into a globally good solution if the vector position of the features is completely randomized within the chromosome any such good performance is lost Optional Reading Minton et al 199 AAAI Classic Paper Award recipient in 2 8 How to solve the 1 Million Queens problem and schedule space telescopes Optional Lecture Slides Review Word PDF a collection of student coding resources is available The coding resources include 1 A Java shell 2 A C shell 3 A tournament shell which will let you play different versions of your AI against themselves to refine your evaluation function 4 Three example AIs which you or your AI can play against a good AI an average AI and a poor AI 5 The DummyAI source code which your cleverness and ingenuity will make smart 6 Several readme txt files readme txt readme cPlusPlus txt readme tournament txt 7 ConnectK hints caveats and heuristics 8 A changelog txt Please note We ll run the tournament on SGE or a lab machine The C target platform should be x86 You should write your code to run on any x86 machine The OS is CentOS 6 We most likely will need to compile your code with CentOS 6 RHEL 6 x86 64 Machines in the openlab ics uci edu family guy ics uci edu are CentOS 6 Please note Connect K like most board games of its type has a built in advantage to the first player e g chess grandmasters try to win if they are white and play first they try to draw if they are black and play second A fairer game would have the first player make one move then the second player make two moves then the first player make two moves and so on alternately making two moves each to neutralize the first move advantage The point of this exercise is for you to write a smart AI not to win board games nevertheless be sure to run your AI both as first and second player then average the results Please note The shells may change as the quarter progresses If so we will try to keep the interface the same so that all you need do is change the surrounding shell Several of my various CS 171 projects were written by former CS 171 students who became interested in AI and signed up for CS 199 in order to pursue their interest and write interesting AI project shells Please let me know if this is of interest to you CS 171 grade of A or better required Study Guides Previous CS 171 Quizzes Mid AAAI Innovative Applications of Artificial Intelligence Conference Academic Honesty Academic dishonesty is unacceptable and will not be tolerated at the University of California Irvine It is the responsibility of each student to be familiar with and without exception to adhere to UCI s current academic honesty policies This class has a zero tolerance policy toward academic dishonesty Any student who engages in cheating forgery dishonest conduct plagiarism or collusion in dishonest activities will receive an academic evaluation of F for the entire course with a letter of explanation to the student s permanent file The ICS Student Affairs Office will be involved at every step of the process Please take the time to read the current UCI Senate Academic Honesty Policy UC Irvine Academic Senate Manual Appendix VIII also reproduced in the Appendix of the UCI Catalogue which states among other things Academic dishonesty is unacceptable and will not be tolerated at the University of California Irvine Cheating forgery dishonest conduct plagiarism and collusion in dishonest activities erode the University s educational research and social roles They devalue the learning experience and its legitimacy not only for the perpetrators but for the entire community Please also review the ICS Undergraduate Student Policies Academic Integrity which states among other things Academically Honest Conduct To be academically integrous means holding to values such as honesty fairness respect and accountability in your scholastic pursuits Students are expected to follow the rules and guidelines established by instructors for assignments and exams and to accept responsibility for his or her own work Please also review Academic misconduct at UC Irvine A summary of that information is Any student cited for Academic Misconduct will have the report kept on file for 5 years During this time a second incident report would likely trigger suspension or dismissal from UCI A single incident on file usually also results in the student being ineligible for honors at graduation Many graduate and professional programs request this information and it may affect admission Please also review the UCI Code of Student Conduct Grounds for Discipline which lists among other offenses 1 2 1 All forms of academic misconduct including but not limited to cheating fabrication plagiarism or facilitating academic dishonesty Refer to Academic Senate Policy on Academic Honesty 1 2 2 Other forms of dishonesty including but not limited to fabricating information furnishing false information or reporting a false emergency to the University The policies in all of these documents will be adhered to scrupulously No exceptions We aggressively watch and monitor all Quizzes and Exams All Quizzes and Exams include your row seat ID and ID to right so that we can reconstruct exactly the seating pattern in the exam room We know next to whom you were seated and so we easily can check for suspicious patterns of answers All source code and all written reports are subject to automatic text based plagiarism detection My responsibility is to the honest students who succeed based on their own merit and hard work If you are cheating then we are aggressively out to catch you Penalties are severe The worst part of my job is to have to catch and penalize a cheating student Please do not do this to me or to you Dr Lathrop strives very hard to create a level playing field for all students ", "_id": "http://www.ics.uci.edu/~rickl/courses/cs-171/2015-wq-cs171/CS-171-WQ-2015.htm", "title": Roman\"'>&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>19\r\nFeb 2015: Effective immediately, the project grading structure is changed as\r\nfollows:<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Poor</span>, <span class=SpellE>AI_Average</span>, and <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Good</span> also will be entered into the Final Tournament\r\n(these AIs are available in the &quot;student coding resources&quot; part of\r\nthe Project section of the class website).<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p your AI does not beat or tie <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Poor</span> in the Final Tournament.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p your AI does not beat or tie <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Average</span> in the Final Tournament (total loss of 30% if\r\nyour AI loses to both <span class=SpellE>AI_Poor</span> and <span class=SpellE>AI_Average</span>).<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* You\r\nwill GAIN 10% BONUS added to your Project grade if your AI beats or ties <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Good</span> in the Final Tournament.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* As\r\npreviously stated, the top 10% in the Final Tournament will receive 10% BONUS,\r\nthe second 10% will receive 9% BONUS, <span class=GramE>the</span> third 10%\r\nwill receive 8% BONUS, and so on.<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span\r\nstyle='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>13 Feb 2015: Happy Friday the 13<sup>th</sup>!!\r\nThe FQ&#8217;2015 Mid-term Exam key has been posted to the class website below,\r\nand also is available any read/permission problems.<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span (the\r\nMid-term Exam), please try to arrive in class and get settled a few minutes\r\nearly. We would like to pass out the Exam quickly, so that you have the maximum\r\namount of time to work on it.<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span\r\nstyle='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>10 Feb 2015: Dr. Lathrop&#8217;s\r\noffice hours are cancelled for Thurs., 12 Feb. (immediately after Mid-term\r\nExam).<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span\r\nstyle='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>4 Feb 2015: A kind and helpful student\r\nhas brought it to my attention that the PDF reader on a Mac (iPad) sometimes\r\nhas difficulty correctly reading the previous CS-171 tests. For example, in\r\nproblems #3a and #3b on Quiz #2 from SQ&#8217;2004, the erroneous\r\n&#8220;Y&#8221; on the key was corrected by an overlay in the PDF file of a red\r\nX through the Y, and next to it a red N. However, this overlay is invisible on\r\na Mac (iPad), leading to incorrect understanding of the right answer.\r\nSometimes, the Mac PDF software appears to be incompatible with the Windows PDF\r\nsoftware. If you are using a Mac to read the previous CS-171 test PDF files and\r\nsomething looks wrong, please look at it again from Windows. If it still looks\r\nwrong, please bring it to my attention.<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span\r\nstyle='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>3 Feb 2015: The Quiz #2 answer key has\r\nbeen posted below and is available <a\r\nhref=\"../cs171-old-tests/2015-wq-cs171-old-tests/2015-wq-cs-171-quiz-2-key.pdf\">here</a>.<span\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span\r\nstyle='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>27 Jan 2015: Michael <span\r\nclass=SpellE>Beyeler</span> has kindly updated ConnectK.cpp and readme.txt,\r\nwhich have been posted to the student coding resources in the Project section\r\nbelow. style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:red'>(If you send email, please\r\nput &#8220;CS-171&#8221; somewhere in the Subject line.)</span><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'> <o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>\r\n\r\n<hr size=2 width=\"100%\" align=left>\r\n\r\n</span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Goal:\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:red'>Goal:</span><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";\r\ncolor:black'>The goal of this class is to familiarize you with the basic\r\nprinciples of artificial intelligence. You will l</span><span style='font-size:\r\n12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>earn <span style='color:black'>some\r\n</span>basic AI techniques, the problems for which they are applicable, and\r\ntheir limitations.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>The\r\ncourse content is organized roughly around what are often considered to be\r\nthree central pillars of AI: Search, Logic, and Learning. Topics covered\r\ninclude basic search, heuristic search, game playing, constraint satisfaction,\r\nknowledge representation, logic and inference, probabilistic modeling, and\r\nmachine learning algorithms.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>This is a broad\r\nintroductory survey course. We will move rapidly through the basic fundamentals\r\nof a large number of AI topics. For every topic that we touch, there are\r\nspecialized techniques available to the sophisticated practitioner that will go\r\nbeyond what we are able to cover in 10 short weeks. The bright, interested, and\r\nmotivated student is encouraged to pursue advanced studies. In any case, if you\r\nwork hard, study hard, and master the presented material, you will emerge from\r\nthis course with a basic grasp of some of the fundamental methods that we use\r\nto engineer intelligent systems.</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'> </span></b><span style='mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<div class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>\r\n\r\n<hr size=2 width=\"100%\" align=center>\r\n\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Class_Setup:\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:red'>Class Setup:</span><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>The\r\ncourse will be primarily lecture-based.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>There will be a Mid-term and a Final Exam.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>On most second Tuesdays, the first 20\r\nminutes will be an in-class pop quiz, followed by lecture (see specific dates\r\nin <a href=\"#_Syllabus:\">Syllabus below</a>).<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>The frequent quizzes are intended to\r\nencourage you to stay current with the course material.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span><u>All exams and quizzes may cover all\r\nmaterial presented in class, including lectures and assigned textbook reading.</u><span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Quizzes will cover mostly material\r\npresented since the last quiz, and also may include questions that many\r\nstudents missed on the previous quiz.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>The Final Exam will cover mostly material since the Mid-term Exam, and\r\nalso will include many questions intended to encourage you to remember the\r\nearlier material (i.e., it will be comprehensive). <u>Please study the previous\r\nCS-171 quizzes and exams (<a href=\"#_Study_Guides_---\">below</a>), which are\r\nmade available as study guides to help you learn and master the class material;\r\nthey are important guides about the performance that will be expected from you\r\nnow.</u><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>There\r\nwill be an AI coding project (see <a href=\"#_Project:_1\">Project section below</a>).<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>You are allowed to do the project by\r\nyourself, or you may form project teams of two students following the &#8220;<a\r\nhref=\"http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pair_programming\">Pair Programming</a>&#8221;\r\nparadigm.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Please note that you are\r\nencouraged to discuss concepts, methods, algorithms, etc.; but you are\r\nforbidden to copy: (1) source code from any source, or (2) text from any source\r\nunless properly cited and set off as a quote.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Except for class materials provided from\r\nthis class website, you must invent and write all of your own code by yourself\r\nwith your partner.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Except for\r\nproperly referenced material, you must write all of your own project report by\r\nyourself with your partner. Please note that your source code and project\r\nreport are subject to analysis by automated plagiarism detection programs, and\r\nthat direct copying will be treated as an act of academic dishonesty (please\r\nsee the section on &#8220;<a href=\"#_Academic_Honesty:\">Academic Honesty</a>&#8221;\r\nbelow). Please start your AI coding project earlier than you believe necessary;\r\nit will take longer and be more difficult than you expect (<u>as is true of all\r\ncoding projects everywhere at all times</u>).<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>All\r\nmy AI project shells were written by former CS-171 students who became\r\ninterested in AI and signed up for CS-199 in order to pursue their interest and\r\nwrite more interesting AI project shells.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>Please let me know if this is of interest to you (CS-171 grade of A- or\r\nbetter required).<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>Homework\r\nwill be assigned, but is not graded. The reason is that prior student course\r\nevaluations alerted me to the existence of student cheating by way of copying\r\nthe homework answers.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>I deplore\r\nthis degree of personal degradation in dishonest students, but I cannot control\r\nit, and so I avoid the opportunity.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>I remain determined to create a fair and honest educational experience\r\nfor all students, as best I can.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";color:black'>\r\n\r\n<hr size=2 width=\"100%\" align=left>\r\n\r\n</span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Textbook\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:red'>Textbook</span><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";\r\ncolor:red'>Required:</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";color:black'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>Russell &amp; <span class=SpellE><span class=GramE>Norvig</span></span><span\r\nclass=GramE> :</span> Artificial Intelligence; A Modern Approach, 3<sup>rd</sup>\r\nedition.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p><span style='mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:black'>The\r\ncourse is based on, and the UCI bookstore has, the 3<sup>rd</sup> edition. </span>The final exam will\r\ncover all course material from the entire quarter, with emphasis on the second\r\nhalf.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span><u>It is not possible to\r\nmake-up a missed final exam.<o:p></o:p></u></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>*\r\nfield maneuvers of the US military or National Guard (<u>I require a copy of\r\nyour official orders</u>).<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'>Also, I honor all requests made by the <a\r\nhref=\"http://www.disability.uci.edu/\">UCI Disability Services Center</a>.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;\r\nmso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;font-weight:normal;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><span\r\nstyle='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'>The AI coding project will be a Connect-K Game\r\ncontroller.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>This project corresponds\r\nto Game/Adversarial Search (Chapter 5 in your book). Your job is to write an AI\r\nagent that can beat you at Connect-K, i.e., to write the adversarial search\r\n(game search) controller for a game-playing agent. <o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'>I expect to be able to run a tournament within which your AI\r\ncontrollers will compete against each other for Bonus Points. Everyone&#8217;s\r\nAI will be entered into the tournament automatically; the bonus points are\r\nsimply free, based on how many games your AI wins against other AIs. The top\r\n10% winners will get 10% added to their project grade as a bonus; the second\r\n10% will get 9%; the third 10% will get 8%; and so on.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if align=center>\r\n\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Study_Habits:\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\r\n\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:red'>Study\r\nHabits:</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>This\r\ncourse is technical, rigorous, and demanding. You will be expected to learn and\r\nmaster a large body of technical material in a very short period of <span\r\nclass=GramE>time,</span> and to demonstrate your mastery by (1) accurate\r\nperformance on frequent quizzes and exams, and (2) successful implementation of\r\nan AI coding project.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>Although\r\nI deliberately treat you as adults who are responsible for your own educational\r\ndecisions, and so lecture and discussion sections are optional ---\r\nnevertheless, students who do not attend lecture or discussion sections are at\r\na serious disadvantage and do not succeed as well in this class.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>They send me emails asking questions\r\nthat already were covered thoroughly and in detail during lecture and again in\r\ndiscussion section.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>They miss\r\npoints on quizzes and exams that already have been discussed thoroughly. <u>Your\r\neducational moments are precious, and your education now will be the single\r\nmost important factor in your future career success or failure.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Please, make the most of your precious\r\neducational moments now; please, attend both lecture and discussion section.</u><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>Please\r\ndo not ever fall behind in the class material; instead, <u>study frequently and\r\ndiligently</u>. Please begin your AI coding project earlier than you believe\r\nnecessary; it will take longer and be more difficult than you expect (<u>as is\r\ntrue of all coding projects everywhere at all times</u>).<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>Please\r\nwork harder and study longer.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>Please understand thoroughly all class material, and ask questions when\r\nyou do not understand.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Please\r\nattend all lectures and discussion sections.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Please come to lectures and discussion\r\nsections prepared with questions about any material that is not clear.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Please do all assigned reading, both\r\nbefore and again after lecture. Please review the lecture notes, several times\r\nover, both before and again after lecture, until you understand every detail.\r\nPlease regularly attend office hours with me and the TA. Please ask questions\r\nabout any class material that is not absolutely crystal clear.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'>Please\r\n<u>work and understand all past quizzes and exams; they are important guides\r\nabout the performance that will be expected from you now.</u> Please work and\r\nunderstand all the optional homework.<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New </span>Eric\r\ncomments, &#8220;One thing to possibly discuss with the last slide is that the\r\nitinerary it settles on does stay at a higher energy for a little bit until it\r\npasses closest to Europa, maximizing the velocity before the insertion sequence\r\nto the lower energy.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>This is indeed\r\noptimal behavior, as opposed to immediately reducing its energy as a Greedy\r\nBest First algorithm using this heuristic would want to do.&#8221; <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:black'><span\r\nstyle='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>(2)\r\nRepresentation [<a href=\"../cs171-lecture-slides/cs-171-02-A-Representation.pdf\">PDF</a>;\r\n<a href=\"../cs171-lecture-slides/cs-171-02-A-Representation.pptx\">PPT</a>].<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Optional URLs:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;<a\r\nhref=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simulated_annealing#mediaviewer/File:Hill_Climbing_with_Simulated_Annealing.gif\">Hill\r\nClimbing with Simulated Annealing</a>&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;<a\r\nhref=\"http://www.boxcar2d.com/\">Boxcar 2D</a>&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:\r\n3'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The\r\nprogram learns to build a car using a genetic algorithm.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:\r\n3'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>If\r\nyou let this program run for a long time (&gt;&gt; 30 generations), you will\r\nsee that eventually it produces cars well suited to the terrain. This outcome\r\nillustrates a general theme of genetic algorithms: very, very slow; but,\r\neventually, good performance. After all, it took ~3.6 billion years to evolve\r\nhumans from bacteria (<a\r\nhref=\"http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Timeline_of_evolutionary_history_of_life\">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Timeline_of_evolutionary_history_of_life</a>).\r\nPlease note that this eventual good performance of genetic algorithms is conditional\r\nupon a representation that allows good solutions to sub-problems to be combined\r\nsimply, by cross-over, into a globally good solution; if the vector position of\r\nthe features is completely randomized within the chromosome, any such good\r\nperformance is lost.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:\r\n2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:\r\n1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Optional\r\nReading:<br>\r\n<span style='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Minton,\r\n<span class=GramE>et</span>. <span class=GramE>al., 1990,<span\r\nstyle='color:#0033BB'> </span><span style='color:black'><a\r\nhref=\"http://www.aaai.org/Papers/AAAI/1990/AAAI90-003.pdf\">AAAI &quot;Classic\r\nPaper&quot; Award recipient in 2008</a>.</span></span><span style='color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:black'><span\r\nstyle='mso-tab-count:3'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Lathrop.</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt'> <o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt'><span\r\nstyle='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span\r\nclass=GramE><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>&#8220;<a\r\nhref=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Technological_singularity\">Technological\r\nsingularity</a>&#8221; --- Wikipedia.</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-1.5in'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;The\r\ntechnological singularity hypothesis is that accelerating progress in\r\ntechnologies will cause a runaway effect wherein artificial intelligence will\r\nexceed human intellectual capacity and control, thus radically changing or even\r\nending civilization in an event called the singularity.&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span\r\nclass=GramE>&#8220;<a\r\nhref=\"http://www-rohan.sdsu.edu/faculty/vinge/misc/singularity.html\">The Coming\r\nTechnological Singularity: How to Survive in the Post-Human Era</a>&#8221; (c)\r\n1993 by <span class=SpellE>Vernor</span> <span class=SpellE>Vinge</span>.</span><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:3'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>(Verbatim\r\ncopying/translation and distribution of this entire article <span class=GramE>is</span>\r\npermitted in any medium, provided this notice is preserved.)<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-1.5in'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;Abstract:<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Within thirty years,\r\nwe will have the technological means to create superhuman intelligence. Shortly\r\nafter, the human era will be ended.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>Is such progress avoidable? If not to be avoided, can events be guided\r\nso that we may survive?<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>These\r\nquestions are investigated. Some possible answers (and some further dangers)\r\nare presented.&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-1.5in'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;....\r\nJust so I'm not guilty of a relative-time ambiguity, let me more specific: I'll\r\nbe surprised if this event occurs before 2005 or after 2030....&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:2'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span\r\nclass=GramE>Rumors,</span> and rumors of rumors.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>You get to make up your own mind.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>;-)<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:.5in'><span style='color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><a name=\"_Draft_Project_Deadline:\"></a><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\"'>Draft Project Deadline:<o:p></o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; class=MsoNormal><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Project:_1\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\ncolor:red'>Project:</span><span class=MsoHyperlink><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:windowtext;font-weight:normal;\r\ntext-decoration:none;text-underline:none'><o:p></o:p></span></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span class=GramE><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;\r\nbackground:yellow;mso-highlight:yellow'>Connect-K Game.</span></b></span><b><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";\r\nmso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>This project corresponds to Game Search (Chapter 5 in your book). Your\r\njob is to write an AI agent that can beat you at Connect-K, i.e., to write the adversarial\r\nsearch (game search) controller for a video game world. Shells are available in\r\nC++ and Java.</span></b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>The tournament shell\r\nwill allow you to run different versions of your AI against each other, or\r\nagainst your fellow students&#8217; AIs, to explore which &#8220;great\r\nideas&#8221; make things better or worse. Bright and clever students might\r\nimplement a Local Search method (perhaps using genetic algorithms?) to explore\r\ndifferent improvements to their AI automatically, while they sleep?<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>I expect to be able to\r\nrun a tournament within which your AI controllers will compete against each\r\nother for Bonus Points. Everyone&#8217;s AI will be entered into the tournament\r\nautomatically; the bonus points are simply free, based on how many games your\r\nAI wins against other AIs. The top 10% winners will get 10% added to their\r\nproject grade as a bonus; the second 10% will get 9%; the third 10% will get\r\n8%; and so on.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>v<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Effective\r\nimmediately, the project grading structure is changed as follows:<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Poor</span>, <span class=SpellE>AI_Average</span>, and <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Good</span> also will be entered into the Final Tournament\r\n(these AIs are available in the &quot;student coding resources&quot; part of\r\nthe Project section of the class website).<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* You\r\nwill lose 20% of your Project grade if your AI does not beat or tie <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Poor</span> in the Final Tournament.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* You\r\nwill lose 10% of your Project grade if your AI does not beat or tie <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Average</span> in the Final Tournament (total loss of 30% if\r\nyour AI loses to both <span class=SpellE>AI_Poor</span> and <span class=SpellE>AI_Average</span>).<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* You\r\nwill GAIN 10% BONUS added to your Project grade if your AI beats or ties <span\r\nclass=SpellE>AI_Good</span> in the Final Tournament.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.5in;\r\nmargin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>* As\r\npreviously stated, the top 10% in the Final Tournament will receive 10% BONUS,\r\nthe second 10% will receive 9% BONUS, <span class=GramE>the</span> third 10%\r\nwill receive 8% BONUS, and so on.<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New <a\r\nhref=\"../../AI-projects/connect-k/Connect-K-report-template.pdf\">PDF</a>].<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(1) A Java shell.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New of your AI against themselves to\r\nrefine your evaluation function.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(4) Three example AIs,\r\nwhich you or your AI can play against: a good AI, an average AI, and a poor AI.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(5) The &#8220;<span\r\nclass=SpellE>DummyAI</span>&#8221; source code, which your cleverness and\r\ningenuity will make smart.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(6) Several readme*.txt\r\nfiles: readme.txt, readme-cPlusPlus.txt, <span class=GramE>readme</span>-tournament.txt.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(7) <span class=SpellE>ConnectK</span>\r\nhints, caveats, and heuristics.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>(8) A changelog.txt.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;background:yellow;\r\nmso-highlight:yellow'>Please note:</span></b><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>\r\nWe'll run the tournament on SGE or a lab machine. The C++ target platform\r\nshould be x86. You should write your code to run on any x86 <span class=GramE>machine</span>.\r\nThe OS is CentOS 6. We most likely will need to compile your code with CentOS 6\r\n(RHEL 6) x86_64. Machines in the openlab.ics.uci.edu (family-guy.ics.uci.edu)\r\nare CentOS 6.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;background:yellow;\r\nmso-highlight:yellow'>Please note:</span></b><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>\r\nConnect-K, like most board games of its type, has a built-in advantage to the\r\nfirst player (e.g., chess grandmasters try to win if they are white and play\r\nfirst; they try to draw if they are black and play second). A\r\n&#8220;fairer&#8221; game would have the first player make one move; then the\r\nsecond player make two moves; then the first player make two moves; and so on,\r\nalternately making two moves each, to neutralize the first-move advantage. The\r\npoint of this exercise is for you to write a &#8220;smart&#8221; AI, not to win\r\nboard games; nevertheless, be sure to run your AI both as first and second\r\nplayer, then average the results.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;background:yellow;\r\nmso-highlight:yellow'>Please note:</span></b><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>\r\nThe shells may change as the quarter progresses.<span\r\nstyle='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>If so, we will try to keep the interface\r\nthe same, so that all you need do is change the surrounding shell.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\r\n\"Times New Roman\";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>Several of my various\r\nCS-171 projects were written by former CS-171 students who became interested in\r\nAI and signed up for CS-199 in order to pursue their interest and write\r\ninteresting AI project shells.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;\r\n</span>Please let me know if this is of interest to you (CS-171 grade of A- or\r\nbetter required).</span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b name=\"_Study_Guides_---\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\r\n\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:red'>Study Guides --- Previous CS-171 Quizzes,\r\nMid-term, and Final exams:</span><span class=MsoHyperlink><span\r\nstyle='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";color:windowtext;\r\nfont-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;text-underline:none'><o:p></o:p></span></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Previous\r\nCS-171 Quizzes, Mid-term exams, and Final exams are available here as study\r\nguides.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>As an\r\nincentive to study this material, at least one question from a previous Quiz or\r\nExam will appear on every new Quiz or Exam. In particular, questions that many\r\nstudents missed are likely to appear again. If you missed a question, please\r\nstudy it carefully and learn from your mistake --- so that if it appears again,\r\nyou will understand it perfectly. <o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Also, a\r\nstudent has recommended &#8216;quizlet.com&#8217; as a good online study\r\nresource. While I cannot vouch for it, apparently it contains several good\r\nstudy aids for your textbook.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>A kind and\r\nhelpful student has brought it to my attention that the PDF reader on a Mac\r\n(iPad) sometimes has difficulty correctly reading the previous CS-171 tests.\r\nFor example, in problems #3a and #3b on Quiz #2 from SQ&#8217;2004, the\r\nerroneous &#8220;Y&#8221; on the key was corrected by an overlay in the PDF\r\nfile of a red X through the Y, and next to it a red N. However, this overlay is\r\ninvisible on a Mac (iPad), leading to incorrect understanding of the right\r\nanswer. Sometimes, the Mac PDF software appears to be incompatible with the\r\nWindows PDF software. If you are using a Mac to read the previous CS-171 test\r\nPDF files and something looks wrong, please look at it again from Windows. If\r\nit still looks wrong, please bring it to my attention.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<h2 style='margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;\r\nfont-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\n\r\n<hr size=2 width=\"100%\" align=left>\r\n\r\n</span></h2>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<div>\r\n\r\n<h2><a name=\"_Academic_Honesty:\"></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:\r\n\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:red'>Academic Honesty: </span><span\r\nclass=MsoHyperlink><span style='color:windowtext;text-decoration:none;\r\ntext-underline:none'><o:p></o:p></span></span></h2>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Academic dishonesty is unacceptable\r\nand will not be tolerated at the University of California, Irvine. It is the\r\nresponsibility of each student to be familiar with, and without exception to\r\nadhere to, UCI's current academic honesty policies.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>This class has a &#8220;zero\r\ntolerance&#8221; policy toward academic dishonesty.</span></u></b><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\nAny student who engages in cheating, forgery, dishonest conduct, plagiarism, or\r\ncollusion in dishonest activities, will receive an academic evaluation of ``F''\r\nfor the entire course, with a letter of explanation to the student's permanent\r\nfile. The <a href=\"http://www.ics.uci.edu/grad/sao/index.php\">ICS Student\r\nAffairs Office</a> will be involved at every step of the process.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Please take the time</span></u></b><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\nto read the current <a\r\nhref=\"http://senate.uci.edu/uci-academic-senate-manual-2/part-iii-appendices-of-the-irvine-division/appendix-viii-uci-academic-senate-policy-on-academic-honesty/\">UCI\r\nSenate Academic Honesty Policy (UC Irvine Academic Senate Manual, Appendix\r\nVIII)</a>, also reproduced in the <a\r\nhref=\"http://catalogue.uci.edu/appendix/#academichonestytext\">Appendix of the\r\nUCI Catalogue</a>, which states, among other things:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.5in'><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span\r\nstyle='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;....\r\nAcademic dishonesty is unacceptable and will not be tolerated at the University\r\nof California, Irvine. Cheating, forgery, dishonest conduct, plagiarism, and\r\ncollusion in dishonest activities erode the University&#8217;s educational,\r\nresearch, and social roles. They devalue the learning experience and its\r\nlegitimacy not only for the perpetrators but for the entire\r\ncommunity....&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Please also review</span></u></b><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\nthe <a href=\"https://www.ics.uci.edu/ugrad/policies/Academic_Integrity.php\">ICS\r\nUndergraduate Student Policies: Academic Integrity</a>, which states, among\r\nother things:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.5in'><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><span\r\nstyle='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>&#8220;Academically\r\nHonest Conduct:<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>To be academically <span\r\nclass=SpellE>integrous</span> means holding to values such as honesty,\r\nfairness, respect, and accountability in your scholastic pursuits. Students are\r\nexpected to follow the rules and guidelines established by instructors for\r\nassignments and <span class=GramE>exams,</span> and to accept responsibility\r\nfor his or her own work....&#8221;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Please also review</span></u></b><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\n<a href=\"http://honesty.uci.edu/\">Academic misconduct at UC Irvine</a>. A\r\nsummary of that information is: <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Any student cited for Academic\r\nMisconduct will have the report kept on file for 5 years.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>During this time, a second incident\r\nreport would likely trigger suspension or dismissal from UCI.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>A single incident on file usually also\r\nresults in the student being ineligible for honors at graduation.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Many graduate and professional\r\nprograms request this information and it may affect admission.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Please also review</span></u></b><b\r\nstyle='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>\r\nthe <a\r\nhref=\"http://www.dos.uci.edu/conduct/students/code-of-student-conduct-grounds-for-discipline.php\">UCI\r\nCode of Student Conduct: Grounds for Discipline</a>, which lists, among other\r\noffenses:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo8'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>102.01: All forms of academic\r\nmisconduct including but not limited to cheating, fabrication, plagiarism, or\r\nfacilitating academic dishonesty. Refer to <a\r\nhref=\"http://senate.uci.edu/uci-academic-senate-manual-2/part-iii-appendices-of-the-irvine-division/appendix-viii-uci-academic-senate-policy-on-academic-honesty/\">Academic\r\nSenate Policy on Academic Honesty</a>.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo8'><![if !supportLists]><span\r\nstyle='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nSymbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt \"Times New Roman\"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\r\n</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>102.02: Other forms of dishonesty\r\nincluding but not limited to fabricating information, furnishing false\r\ninformation, or reporting a false emergency to the University.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";\r\ncolor:red'>The policies in all of these documents will be adhered to\r\n*scrupulously*. No exceptions.</span></u></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>We aggressively watch and monitor all Quizzes\r\nand Exams. All Quizzes and Exams include your row#, seat#, ID#, and\r\nID#-to-right, so that we can reconstruct *exactly* the seating pattern in the\r\nexam room. We know next to whom you were seated, and so we easily can check for\r\nsuspicious patterns of answers.<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>All\r\nsource code and all written reports are subject to automatic text-based\r\nplagiarism detection.</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";mso-fareast-font-family:\"Times New Roman\";\r\nmso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\";color:red'><o:p><span style='text-decoration:\r\n none'>&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></u></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span\r\nstyle='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>My responsibility is to the honest\r\nstudents who succeed based on their own merit and hard work. <u>If you are\r\ncheating, then we are *aggressively* out to catch you. Penalties are severe.</u>\r\nThe worst part of my job is to have to catch and penalize a cheating student.\r\nPlease do not do this to me or to you. <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:\"Arial\",\"sans-serif\"'>Dr.\r\nLathrop strives very hard to create a level playing field for all students.</span></b><span\r\nclass=MsoHyperlink><span
